## Instruction

As a novice video content creator, I want to analyze the video style and patterns of the creator "MrBeast." I'd like to understand when his videos typically generate more traffic and what the optimal video length is.
Please find all MrBeast's videos (longer than two minutes) and analyze publishing patterns from the beginning of 2024 to July 1, 2025. Determine the day of the week with the most frequent video uploads, the average video length, and the average number of days between uploads (calculated based on date differences). 

You also need to categorize them according to the following four classifications:

- **Challenges**: Extreme competitions with specific rules to win huge cash prizes or rewards.
- **Philanthropy**: Large-scale donations and charitable initiatives to help others.
- **Survival**: Personal experience of enduring extended periods in extreme or unfamiliar environments.
- **Comparison Experiments**: Experiments that contrast vastly different prices to observe outcomes.

Populate all results into the existing `result.xlsx` file in the workspace, arranged in chronological order of published date. In the two separate sheets, please fill in the detailed information for the videos from this period and the statistics I've requested, respectively. The specific content to be entered should follow the structure of the `result.xlsx` file, do not edit the headers. Do not create new worksheets without authorization. For `Monday/Tuesday/..._publish_proportion` you should fill in a float from 0 to 1. Please round all decimal numbers to two decimal places.

    ("hTSaweR8qMI", "$1 vs $500,000 Date", "2025-06-07T16:00:00Z", 17*60+22),
    ("pzBi1nwDn8U", "Lose 100 LBs, Win $250,000!", "2025-06-21T16:00:01Z", 36*60+50),
]

# Weekday mapping
weekday_names = ["Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday","Sunday"]

# Sort chronologically
videos_sorted = sorted(videos, key=lambda x: x[2])

# Compute weekdays and intervals
weekdays = []
parsed_dates = []
for vid in videos_sorted:
    dt = datetime.strptime(vid[2], "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ").replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    parsed_dates.append(dt)
    weekdays.append(weekday_names[dt.weekday()])

# Average duration
avg_duration_sec = sum(v[3] for v in videos_sorted)/len(videos_sorted)

# Average interval in days
intervals_days = [(parsed_dates[i+1]-parsed_dates[i]).total_seconds()/86400 for i in range(len(parsed_dates)-1)]
avg_interval_days = sum(intervals_days)/len(intervals_days)

# Weekday counts and proportions
cnt = Counter(weekdays)

total = len(videos_sorted)
proportions = {day: cnt.get(day,0)/total for day in ["Sunday","Saturday","Friday","Thursday","Wednesday","Tuesday","Monday"]}

# Most common weekday
most_common_weekday = max(cnt.items(), key=lambda x: (x[1], x[0]))[0]

# Format avg duration HH:MM:SS
avg_sec_round = int(round(avg_duration_sec))
hh = avg_sec_round//3600
mm = (avg_sec_round%3600)//60
ss = avg_sec_round%60
avg_duration_str = f"{hh:02d}:{mm:02d}:{ss:02d}"

print("count", total)
print("most_common_weekday", most_common_weekday)
print("avg_duration_str", avg_duration_str)
print("avg_interval_days", round(avg_interval_days,2))
print("proportions", {k: round(v,2) for k,v in proportions.items()})
print("weekdays_counts", cnt)

# Also prepare data rows with category assignment
categories = {}
# Manual mapping as discussed
categories = {
    "Pv0iVoSZzN8": "Challenges",
    "F6PqxbvOCUI": "Challenges",
    "U_LlX4t0A9I": "Survival",
    "PWirijQkH4M": "Challenges",
    "KkCXLABwHP0": "Philanthropy",
    "4SNThp0YiU4": "Challenges",
    "UPrkC1LdlLY": "Survival",
    "ndAQfTzlVjc": "Survival",
    "aRcUVhVlSHg": "Survival",
    "snX5YyflrGw": "Challenges",
    "bn0Kh9c4Zv4": "Survival",
    "X4jmbQg41G6zVYxxKph5Y8JVWmw": "Comparison Experiments",
    "0BjlBnfHcHM": "Challenges",
    "gs8qfL9PNac": "Challenges",
    "SM66GDRyIVY": "Philanthropy",
    "sF5LYGgKbUA": "Challenges",
    "nAiKLoCP-kU": "Survival",
    "zajUgQLviwk": "Challenges",
    "aKq8bkY5eTU": "Survival",
    "figrl0aOULs": "Philanthropy",
    "uyiG6uw-6pA": "Challenges",
    "-4GmbBoYQjE": "Survival",
    "DZIASl9q90s": "Challenges",
    "hTSaweR8qMI": "Comparison Experiments",
    "pzBi1nwDn8U": "Challenges",
}

# Build rows
rows = []
for vid in videos_sorted:
    vid_id, title, pub, dur = vid
    dt = datetime.strptime(pub, "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ").replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    wd = weekday_names[dt.weekday()]
    # format duration
    h = dur//3600
    m = (dur%3600)//60
    s = dur%60
    dur_str = f"{h:02d}:{m:02d}:{s:02d}"
    rows.append([vid_id, title, categories.get(vid_id, ""), pub, dur, dur_str, wd])

print("first_row", rows[0])
print("last_row", rows[-1])
 code

    ("figrl0aOULs","Click This Video To Feed 1 Person","2025-04-12T16:00:01Z", 10*60+29),

    ("DZIASl9q90s","Beat Neymar, Win $500,000","2025-05-24T16:00:01Z", 27*60+53),
    ("hTSaweR8qMI","$1 vs $500,000 Date","2025-06-07T16:00:00Z", 17*60+22),
    ("pzBi1nwDn8U","Lose 100 LBs, Win $250,000!","2025-06-21T16:00:01Z", 36*60+50),
]

# Remove accidental double commas
L = [t for t in L if isinstance(t, tuple) and len(t)==4]

# Filter to cutoff <= 2025-07-01 23:59:59Z
cutoff = datetime(2025,7,1,23,59,59,tzinfo=timezone.utc)
L2 = []
for vid in L:
    dt = datetime.strptime(vid[2], "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ").replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    if dt <= cutoff:
        L2.append(vid)

L2.sort(key=lambda x: x[2])

weekday_names = ["Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday","Sunday"]
weekdays = []
parsed = []
for vid in L2:
    dt = datetime.strptime(vid[2], "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ").replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    parsed.append(dt)
    weekdays.append(weekday_names[dt.weekday()])

from statistics import mean
avg_dur = mean([d for _,_,_,d in L2])

intervals = [(parsed[i+1]-parsed[i]).total_seconds()/86400 for i in range(len(parsed)-1)]
avg_interval = mean(intervals)

from collections import Counter
cnt = Counter(weekdays)
most_day = max(cnt.items(), key=lambda x: (x[1], -weekday_names.index(x[0])))[0]

# Proportions by requested order Monday..Sunday? The sheet expects Sunday...Monday order
order = ["Sunday","Saturday","Friday","Thursday","Wednesday","Tuesday","Monday"]
props = {d: cnt.get(d,0)/len(L2) for d in order}

# Format duration HH:MM:SS rounded to nearest second, and round other decimals to 2
avg_dur_sec = int(round(avg_dur))
hh = avg_dur_sec//3600
mm = (avg_dur_sec%3600)//60
ss = avg_dur_sec%60
avg_dur_str = f"{hh:02d}:{mm:02d}:{ss:02d}"

print('count', len(L2))
print('most', most_day)
print('avg_dur', avg_dur_str)
print('avg_interval', round(avg_interval,2))
print('props', {k: round(v,2) for k,v in props.items()})

# Weekday counts debug
print('counts', cnt)
 code

    if dt <= cutoff:
        L2.append((vid[0], vid[1], dt, vid[3]))

weekdays = [weekday_names[v[2].weekday()] for v in L2]

avg_dur = mean([v[3] for v in L2])
intervals_days = [(L2[i+1][2]-L2[i][2]).total_seconds()/86400 for i in range(len(L2)-1)]
avg_interval = mean(intervals_days)

cnt = Counter(weekdays)
most_day = max(cnt.items(), key=lambda x: (x[1], -weekday_names.index(x[0])))[0]
order = ["Sunday","Saturday","Friday","Thursday","Wednesday","Tuesday","Monday"]
props = {d: cnt.get(d,0)/len(L2) for d in order}

avg_sec = int(round(avg_dur))
hh = avg_sec//3600
mm = (avg_sec%3600)//60
ss = avg_sec%60
avg_dur_str = f"{hh:02d}:{mm:02d}:{ss:02d}"

print("count", len(L2))
print("most_day", most_day)
print("avg_dur_str", avg_dur_str)
print("avg_interval", round(avg_interval,2))
print("props", {k: round(v,2) for k,v in props.items()})
print("weekday_counts", cnt)
